<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:6%; text-indent:5%; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Re: Important Information about <B><U>Claims Information Line</U></B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:28pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Dear&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B>THE GABELLI ASSET FUND</B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:28pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Travelers Bond&nbsp;&amp; Specialty Insurance is pleased to announce its <B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-800-842-8496</FONT></FONT></FONT></B> Claims Information Line. This line is designed to provide insureds with an additional resource on how to report claims or those circumstances or events which may become claims. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Policyholders will be able to obtain assistance on the following topics from the Claims Information Line: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">&middot;The information that needs to be included with the claim notice </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">&middot;The address, electronic mail address and/or facsimile number to which the policyholder can send claims related information </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">&middot; Get questions on the claim process answered </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">The Declarations Page of your policy sets forth where you should report claims and claims related information. You should also review the policy&#146;s
reporting requirements to be aware of how much time you have to report a claim to Travelers. The sooner Travelers is notified, the sooner we can become involved in the process and offer assistance to our policyholder. A delay in reporting may result
in all or part of a matter to fall outside of the coverage provided. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">The Claims Information Line should streamline the claim reporting process and
allow policyholders to ask questions on what information is needed as well as other questions which will assist them in working with Travelers. While the Claims Information Line provides policyholders a valuable resource by answering questions and
providing information, the line does not replace the reporting requirements contained in the Policy. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">We hope this improvement to customer service
is something our policyholders will find helps them understand the claim process and provides them a resource for reporting. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Best regards, </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B>Robert J Barlow </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-888-712-7667</FONT></FONT></FONT> and ask for your Risk Management PLUS+ Online representative. It&#146;s that simple. </P>

liability and crime coverages that are specifically customized for your organization. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><U>Instructions for Registration</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;&amp;

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>FIDELITY </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><A NAME="tx897054_4"></A>Coverage A.1. Larceny or Embezzlement </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:14%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Loss resulting directly from <B>Larceny or Embezzlement</B> committed by an <B>Employee</B> acting alone or in collusion with others.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><A NAME="tx897054_5"></A>Coverage A.2. Restoration Expenses </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:14%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B>Restoration Expenses </B>incurred by the Insured and resulting directly from a<B> Computer Violation </B>by an <B>Employee</B>. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>ON PREMISES </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">1.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Loss of <B>Property</B> resulting directly from: </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="14%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">a.</P></TD>

</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="14%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">b.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">theft, false pretenses, or common law or statutory larceny, committed by a person physically present in an office of,
or on the premises of, the Insured at the time the <B>Property </B>was surrendered,<B> </B> </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:14%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">while the
<B>Property</B> is lodged or deposited within offices or premises located anywhere. The premises of a <B>Depository</B> will be deemed premises of the Insured, but solely as respects loss of <B>Certificated Securities</B>. Coverage for<B>
Certificated Securities </B>held by such<B> Depository </B>is<B> </B>limited to the extent of the Insured&#146;s interest therein as effected by the making of appropriate entries on the books and records of such <B>Depository</B>. The Company will
not be liable under Insuring Agreement B for loss in connection with the central handling of securities within the systems established and maintained by any <B>Depository</B> unless the amount of such loss exceeds the amount recoverable or recovered
under any bond or policy or participants&#146; fund insuring the <B>Depository </B>against such loss. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:14%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">This bond does not afford
any coverage in favor of any <B>Depository</B> or exchange or any nominee in whose name is registered any security included within the <B>Depository&#146;s</B> systems. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Direct loss, through any hazard specified in Insuring Agreement B.1. of any <B>Property</B> while such <B>Property
</B>is within any of the Insured&#146;s or an<B> Investment Adviser&#146;s </B>offices and in the possession<B> </B>of any customer of the Insured, any representative of such customer or any <B>Employee</B> whether or not the Insured is liable for
the loss thereof, and provided such loss, at the option of the Insured, is included in the Insured&#146;s proof of loss, but excluding, in any event, loss caused by such customer, any representative of such customer, or any <B>Employee</B>.

<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B><A NAME="tx897054_7"></A>C.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>IN TRANSIT </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Loss of <B>Property</B> (occurring with or without negligence or violence) resulting directly from robbery, larceny, theft, holdup,
mysterious unexplainable disappearance, misplacement, being lost or otherwise made away with, damage thereto or destruction thereof, and loss of subscription, conversion, redemption or deposit privileges through the misplacement or loss of
<B>Property</B>, while the <B>Property</B> is in transit anywhere in the custody of any person or persons acting as <B>Messenger</B>, except while in the mail or with a carrier for hire other than an armored motor vehicle company, for the purpose of
transportation, such transit to begin immediately upon receipt of such <B>Property</B> by the transporting person or persons, and to end immediately upon delivery thereof at destination, but only while the <B>Property</B> is being conveyed. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Loss resulting directly from the Insured having, in good faith, paid or transferred any <B>Property</B> in reliance on any <B>Written,
Original</B>: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:15%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">that </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">bears a handwritten signature material to the validity or enforceability of the <B>Original Written </B>document that
is a<B> Forgery</B>, but only to the extent the<B> Forgery </B>causes the loss; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">is altered, but only to the extent the alteration causes the loss; or </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">is lost or stolen; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

attorney, <B>Guarantee</B>, endorsement, or any items listed in items 1.a. through 1.i. above; or </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">acquired, sold or delivered, given value, extended credit or assumed liability, on the faith of any item listed in
1.a. through 1.d. above, that is a <B>Counterfeit,</B> but only to the extent the <B>Counterfeit</B> causes the loss. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:11%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Actual physical possession, and continued actual physical possession if taken as collateral, of the items listed in 1.a. through 1.j.
above by the Insured, an <B>Investment Adviser</B>, a <B>Custodian</B>, or a Federal or State chartered deposit institution of the Insured is a condition precedent to the Insured&#146;s having relied on the faith of such items. Release or return of
such collateral is an acknowledgment by the Insured that it no longer relies on such collateral. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:11%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Loss resulting directly from the receipt by the Insured, in good faith, of any <B>Counterfeit Money</B> of the United States of America
and its territories and possessions, Canada or any other country, or of <B>Counterfeit </B>money orders denominated in United States or Canadian currency.<B> </B> </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:11%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Reasonable expenses necessarily incurred and paid by the Insured in preparing any covered claim for loss under any Insuring Agreement
covered under this bond, which loss exceeds the Single Loss Deductible Amount applicable to such Insuring Agreement. Such expenses include costs incurred (including necessary wages of <B>Employees</B>) for that part of audits or examinations
performed, whether or not required by State or Federal supervisory authorities and conducted either by such authorities or by independent accountants, by reason of the discovery of loss sustained by the Insured. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:11%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Damages that the Insured becomes legally liable to pay its customers resulting directly from the Insured or an <B>Investment
Adviser</B> having: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">failed to comply with any notice of any customer of the Insured or any authorized representative of such customer to
stop payment on any check or draft made or drawn by such customer; or </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><A NAME="tx897054_15"></A>Coverage I.2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Fraudulent Instructions </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:15%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Loss resulting directly from the Insured or an <B>Investment Adviser</B> having, in good faith, caused a transfer of funds as a result

I.3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Restoration Expenses </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:15%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B>Restoration Expenses </B>incurred by the Insured or an<B> Investment Adviser
</B>and resulting from a <B>Computer Violation </B>by someone other than an<B> Employee</B>. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Loss, including dividends and interest accrued not to exceed 15% of the value of each <B>Item of Deposit</B> that is deposited,

<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">It is a condition precedent to coverage under this Insuring Agreement that the Insured or <B>Investment</B> <B>Adviser </B>hold funds

</B>standard collection procedures have failed. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">This Insuring Agreement applies to Insureds with exchange privileges if all funds

credited to any fund in the exchange program. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>CONSOLIDATION - MERGER - PURCHASE OR ACQUISITION OF ASSETS </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">If the Insured or an <B>Investment Adviser</B>, while this bond is in force, consolidates or merges with, or purchases or acquires
assets, assets under management or liabilities of, or purchases or acquires more than 50% voting stock ownership of another institution (hereinafter referred to as a &#147;Transaction&#148;), coverage under this bond for loss which: </P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">has been caused or will be caused by any employee or employees of such institution; or </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">3.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">has arisen or will arise out of the assets, assets under management or liabilities acquired by the Insured as a result
of such Transaction, </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">is provided as follows: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">a.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Automatic Loss Sustained Coverage </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:21%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">If a Transaction involves assets, assets under management and liabilities in an amount that is more than 25% of the consolidated assets
of all Insureds as of the most recent calendar <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-end</FONT> preceding the date of the Transaction, then coverage of this bond as respects the Transaction will be afforded for a Single Loss that is both discovered
and for which the acts giving rise to the loss occur in their entirety on or after the effective date of the Transaction. This coverage terminates 60 days after the Transaction date, or the termination date of the bond, whichever comes earlier,
unless the Insured provides notice to the Company and obtains the written consent of the Company to extend such coverage beyond said date and, upon obtaining such consent, pays to the Company an additional premium, if required. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">b.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Automatic Discovery Coverage </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:21%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">If a Transaction involves assets, assets under management and liabilities in an amount that is 25% or less of the consolidated assets
of all Insureds as of the most recent calendar <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-end</FONT> preceding the date of the Transaction, then coverage of this bond as respects the Transaction will be afforded for a Single Loss that is discovered on or
after the effective date of the Transaction, for the remainder of the Policy Period as set forth in ITEM 2 of the Declarations, without additional premium being charged and without notice to the Company of the Transaction. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>REPRESENTATION OF INSURED </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">No statement made by or on behalf of the Insured, whether contained in the application or otherwise, is deemed to be a warranty of
anything except that it is true to the best of the knowledge and belief of the person making the statement. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>JOINT INSURED </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">This bond does not indemnify or hold harmless any Insured for loss sustained by an <B>Investment</B> <B>Adviser</B>, or by a
proprietorship, partnership or corporation that is owned, controlled or operated by such<B> </B>Insured, and not named as an Insured hereunder, except as may be provided on a limited basis within General Agreement B., but this paragraph does not
apply to loss sustained by a nominee organized by an Insured hereunder other than a holding company. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">If two or more Insureds are
covered under this bond, the first named Insured will act for all Insureds. Payment by the Company to the first named Insured of loss sustained by any Insured fully releases the Company on account of such loss. If the first named Insured ceases to
be covered under this bond, the Insured next named will thereafter be considered the first named Insured. In the absence of an Insured </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">being specifically next named, the Insured entity having the greatest consolidated
assets of all remaining Insureds then becomes the first named Insured. Knowledge possessed or discovery made by any Insured or <B>Investment Adviser</B> constitutes knowledge or discovery by all Insureds for all purposes of this bond. The liability
of the Company for loss or losses sustained by all Insureds will not exceed the amount for which the Company would have been liable had all such loss or losses been sustained by one Insured. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>COURT COSTS AND ATTORNEY&#146;S FEES - LEGAL PROCEEDINGS - ELECTION TO DEFEND </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">The Company will indemnify the Insured against court costs and reasonable attorney&#146;s fees incurred and paid by the Insured in
defending any suit or legal proceeding brought against the Insured to enforce the Insured&#146;s liability, or alleged liability, on account of any loss, claim or damage that, if established against the Insured, would constitute a collectible loss
under this bond in excess of any Single Loss Deductible Amount, provided, however, that with respect to Insuring Agreement A this indemnity will apply only in the event that: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="16%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">1.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">an <B>Employee</B> admits to being guilty of <B>Larceny or Embezzlement</B>; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="16%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">2.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">an <B>Employee</B> is adjudicated to be guilty of <B>Larceny or Embezzlement</B>; or </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="16%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">3.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">in the absence of 1. or 2. above, an arbitration panel agrees, after a review of an agreed statement of facts, that an
<B>Employee</B> would be found guilty of <B>Larceny or</B> <B>Embezzlement </B>if such<B> Employee </B>were prosecuted.<B> </B> </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Such indemnity is in addition to the Single Loss Limit of Insurance for the applicable Insuring Agreement or Coverage. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">The Insured or an <B>Investment Adviser</B> must notify the Company promptly after notice thereof, of any such suit or legal proceeding
and at the request of the Company will furnish it with copies of all pleadings and other papers therein. At the Company&#146;s election the Insured will permit the Company to conduct the defense of such suit or legal proceeding, in the
Insured&#146;s name, through attorneys of the Company&#146;s selection. In such event, the Insured and <B>Investment Adviser</B> will give all reasonable information and assistance, other than pecuniary, that the Company deems necessary to the
defense of such suit or legal proceeding. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">If the amount of the Insured&#146;s liability or alleged liability is greater than the
amount recoverable under this bond, or if a Single Loss Deductible Amount is applicable, or both, then the liability of the Company under this General Agreement E. is limited to the proportion of court costs and attorney&#146;s fees incurred and
paid by the Insured or by the Company that the amount recoverable under this bond bears to the total amount of the Insured&#146;s liability or alleged liability. Any amount not recoverable by reason of the Insured&#146;s liability or alleged
liability being greater than the amount recoverable under any insuring agreement of this bond, does not serve to reduce the Single Loss Deductible Amount applicable to such Insuring Agreement or Coverage. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">If the Company pays court costs and attorney&#146;s fees in excess of its proportionate share of such costs and fees, the Insured will
promptly reimburse the Company for such excess. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Certificate of Origin or Title </I></B>means a<B><I> </I></B><B>Written</B><B><I> </I></B>document issued

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Certificated Security </I></B>means a share, participation or other interest in property of, or an
enterprise of, the<B><I> </I></B>issuer or an obligation of the issuer, that is: </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">1.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">represented by a <B>Written</B> instrument issued in bearer or registered form; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">2.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">of a type commonly dealt in on securities exchanges or markets or commonly recognized in any area in which it is
issued or dealt in as a medium for investment; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">3.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">either one of a class or series or by its terms divisible into a class or series of shares, participations, interests
or obligations. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>G.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Computer Fraud </I></B>means an intentional, unauthorized, and fraudulent entry of data or computer<B><I>
</I></B>instructions directly into, or change of data or computer instructions within, a <B>Computer System</B> by a natural person or entity other than an <B>Employee</B>, including any such entry or change made via the internet or a
<B>Network</B>, provided that such entry or change causes: </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">1.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>Property </B>to be transferred, paid, or delivered;<B> </B> </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">2.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">an account of the Insured, or of its customer, to be added, deleted, debited or credited; or </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">3.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">an unauthorized or fictitious account to be debited or credited. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>H.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Computer System </I></B>means:<B><I> </I></B> </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">1.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">any computer; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">2.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">any input, output, processing, storage or communication device, or any related network, operating system or
application software, that is connected to, or used in connection with, such computer, </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">that is rented by, owned
by, leased by, licensed to, or under the direct operational control of, the Insured or an <B>Investment Adviser</B>. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>I.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Computer Violation </I></B>means:<B><I> </I></B> </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">1.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">the introduction of a <B>Computer Virus</B> into a <B>Computer System</B>; or </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">2.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">damage to, or destruction of, computer programs, software or other electronic data stored within a <B>Computer System
</B>by a natural person, who has:<B> </B> </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">a.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">gained unauthorized access to such <B>Computer System</B>; or </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">b.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">authorized access to such <B>Computer System</B> but uses such access to cause such damage or destruction.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>J.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Computer Virus </I></B>means any malicious code that could destroy, alter, contaminate, or degrade
the<B><I> </I></B>integrity, quality, or performance of: </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">1.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">electronic data used, or stored, in any <B>Computer System</B> or network; or </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">2.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">a computer network, any computer application software, or a computer operating system or related network.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>K.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Counterfeit </I></B>means a<B><I> </I></B><B>Written</B><B><I> </I></B>imitation of an actual, valid, or
verifiable<B><I> </I></B><B>Original</B><B><I> </I></B>that is intended to<B><I> </I></B>deceive and to be taken as the <B>Original</B>. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Customer </I></B>means, only with respect to Insuring Agreement I.2., an entity or natural person that

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Depository </I></B>means a clearing corporation that is:<B><I> </I></B> </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">1.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">registered with the Securities Exchange Commission as a clearing agency under section 17A of the Securities Exchange
Act of 1934 (15 U.S.C. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">78q-1);</FONT> or </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">2.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">a Federal Reserve Bank or other person or entity authorized to operate the federal book entry system described in the
regulations of the Department of Treasury codified at 31 CFR 357, Subpart B, or book-entry systems operated pursuant to comparable regulations of other federal agencies. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>O.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Document of Title </I></B>means a<B><I> </I></B><B>Written</B><B><I> </I></B>document that is a bill of
lading, dock warrant, dock receipt,<B><I> </I></B>warehouse receipt or order for the delivery of goods, and also any other <B>Written</B> document that in the regular course of business or financing is treated as adequately evidencing that the
person in possession of it is entitled to receive, hold and dispose of the document and the goods it covers and must purport to be issued by or addressed to a bailee and purport to cover goods in the bailee&#146;s possession that are either
identified or are fungible portions of an identified mass. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>P.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Electronic Data Processor </I></B>means a natural person, partnership or corporation authorized in
writing by<B><I> </I></B>the Insured or an <B>Investment Adviser</B> to perform services as a data processor of checks presented to the Insured by a customer or <B>Financial Institution</B>, but excluding any such processor who acts as a transfer
agent or in any other agency capacity in issuing checks, drafts or securities for the Insured, A Federal Reserve Bank or clearinghouse will not be construed to be an <B>Electronic Data Processor</B>. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>Q.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Electronic Record </I></B>means information that is created, generated, sent, communicated, received,
or<B><I> </I></B>stored by electronic means, and is retrievable in perceivable form. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>R.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Employee </I></B>means:<B><I> </I></B> </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">an officer, partner or other employee of the Insured, while such person is employed by and performing services for the
Insured, and whom the Insured directly compensates by wages, salaries or commissions; or for 60 days after such individual&#146;s termination of service, provided such termination is not due to employee fraud or dishonesty; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">a guest student or intern pursuing studies or duties in any of the Insured&#146;s or an <B>Investment</B>
<B>Adviser&#146;s </B>offices or premises covered hereunder, while such person is performing services for<B> </B>the Insured; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">any attorney retained by the Insured or an <B>Investment Adviser</B>, and any employee of such attorney, but only
while performing legal services for the Insured; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">any natural person assigned to perform the usual duties of an employee within the premises of the Insured or an
<B>Investment Adviser</B> and under the Insured&#146;s supervision, by contract, including such persons provided by any employment agency furnishing temporary personnel to the Insured or an <B>Investment Adviser</B> on a contingent or part-time
basis, and including a natural person who is leased to the Insured or an <B>Investment Adviser</B> under a written agreement between the Insured and a labor leasing firm to perform duties related to the conduct of the Insured&#146;s business; (all
such natural persons provided by a single employment agency or labor leasing firm will collectively be deemed to be one person for all the purposes of this bond, excepting, however, the last paragraph of Condition R.2.); </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">an employee of an institution merged or consolidated with the Insured prior to the effective date of this bond, or,

bank, will be included within the definition of Employee. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B>Employee </B>also means any natural person described above while such
person is on medical, military, or<B> </B>other leave of absence. Coverage applies to any such <B>Employee</B> while on leave, regardless of whether such person remains subject to the Insured&#146;s direction and control during the time of leave.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B>Employee </B>does not mean any agent, broker, factor, commission merchant, consignee, independent<B> </B>contractor or
representative or other person of the same general character not specified above. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">provided that <B>Financial Institution</B> does not include any such entity,
institution or organization that is an Insured or an <B>Investment Adviser</B>. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>U.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Forgery </I></B>means signing the name of another person or organization with a handwritten signature
directly<B><I> </I></B>applied to a <B>Written</B> document without authority, and with the intent to deceive. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">A
signature written on an electronic pad that captures the signature for purposes of creating an electronic digitized image of a handwritten signature, or a reproduction of a handwritten signature, is treated the same as a handwritten signature. Any
other form of electronic signature or digital signature is not treated the same as a handwritten signature. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B>Forgery </B>does
not mean a signature that consists in whole or in part of one&#146;s own name signed with or<B> </B>without authority, in any capacity, for any purpose. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>V.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Fraudulent Instruction </I></B>means an intentional, fraudulent and unauthorized instruction directed to
the<B><I> </I></B>Insured or an <B>Investment Adviser</B>, that is: </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">1.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">transmitted via telefacsimile, and: </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">a.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">purports and reasonably appears to be from a <B>Customer</B>, a <B>Financial Institution</B>, or another office of the
Insured; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">b.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">was in fact transmitted by someone other than a <B>Customer</B>, a <B>Financial Institution</B>, or another office of
the Insured; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">c.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">purports and reasonably appears to contain the handwritten signature of a person authorized to initiate such transfer
that proves to have been used by an unauthorized person; or </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">2.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">transmitted verbally, via telephone, and purports to be from: </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">a.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">an officer, director, partner or employee of a <B>Customer</B>, who is authorized by the <B>Customer </B>to instruct
the Insured or an<B> Investment Adviser </B>to make such a transfer;<B> </B> </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">b.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">a <B>Customer</B> who is a natural person; or </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">c.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">an <B>Employee</B> in another office of the Insured who was authorized by the Insured to instruct other
<B>Employees</B> to transfer funds on deposit in a <B>Customer&#146;s</B> account; and was received by an <B>Employee</B> specifically designated to receive and act upon such instructions, </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:15%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">but was in fact transmitted by someone other than a person described in paragraph V.2.; or </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">3.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">transmitted via electronic mail and purports and reasonably appears to be from a <B>Customer</B> of the Insured, but
was in fact transmitted by someone other than such <B>Customer</B>. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B>Fraudulent Instruction </B>does not
include any instruction that purports to be from a<B> Customer </B>unless the<B> </B>instruction is transmitted by a method that is authorized in the <B>Funds Transfer Agreement</B> between the Insured and the <B>Customer</B>. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>W.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Funds Transfer Agreement </I></B>means an agreement, signed by the<B><I> </I></B><B>Customer</B>,
that:<B><I> </I></B> </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">a.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">authorizes the Insured or an <B>Investment Adviser</B> to rely on instructions transmitted by either voice,
telefacsimile or electronic mail to make funds transfers; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">b.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">provides the Insured or an <B>Investment Adviser</B> with the names of persons authorized to initiate funds transfers.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>X.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Guarantee </I></B>means a<B><I> </I></B><B>Written</B> undertaking obligating the signer to pay the debt
of another to the Insured or its assignee or to a <B>Financial Institution</B> from which the Insured has purchased participation in the debt, if the debt is not paid in accordance with its terms. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>Y.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Instruction </I></B>means a<B><I> </I></B><B>Written</B><B><I> </I></B>order to the issuer of an<B><I>
</I></B><B>Uncertificated Security</B><B><I> </I></B>requesting that the<B><I> </I></B>transfer, pledge, or release from pledge of the <B>Uncertificated Security</B> specified be registered. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>Z.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Investment Adviser </I></B>means any entity defined in &#167;202(a)(11) of, and registered under, the
Investment<B><I> </I></B>Advisers Act of 1940, as amended, but only while acting on behalf of the Insured. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>AA.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Item of Deposit </I></B>means any checks or drafts deposited into the account of a customer, shareholder
or<B><I> </I></B>subscriber. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>BB.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Larceny or Embezzlement </I></B>means larceny or embezzlement as defined in the Investment Company
Act<B><I> </I></B>of 1940, &#167;37 as amended. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>CC.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Letter of Credit </I></B>means an engagement in writing by a<B><I> </I></B><B>Financial
Institution</B><B><I> </I></B>or other person made at the<B><I> </I></B>request of a customer that the <B>Financial Institution</B> or other person will honor drafts or other demands for payment upon compliance with the conditions specified in the
<B>Letter of Credit</B>. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>DD.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Loan </I></B>means all extensions of credit by the Insured and all transactions creating a creditor
relationship in<B><I> </I></B>favor of the Insured and all transactions by which the Insured assumes an existing creditor relationship. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>EE.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Messenger </I></B>means an<B><I> </I></B><B>Employee</B><B><I> </I></B>while in possession of the
Insured&#146;s<B><I> </I></B><B>Property</B><B><I> </I></B>away from the Insured&#146;s<B><I> </I></B>or <B>Investment Adviser&#146;s</B> premises and any other natural person acting as custodian of the <B>Property</B> during an emergency arising
from the incapacity of the original <B>Employee</B>. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>FF.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Money </I></B>means a medium of exchange in current use authorized or adopted by a domestic or
foreign<B><I> </I></B>government as a part of its currency. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>GG.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Negotiable Instrument </I></B>means a<B><I> </I></B><B>Written</B><B><I> </I></B>document, that:<B><I>
</I></B> </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">1.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">is signed by the maker or drawer; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">2.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">contains an unconditional promise or order to pay a sum certain in <B>Money</B> and no other promise, order,
obligation or power given by the maker or drawer; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">3.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">is payable on demand or at a definite time; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">4.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">is payable to order or bearer. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B>Negotiable Instrument </B>also means a counterfeit check or<B> Substitute Check</B>. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>HH.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Network </I></B>means any and all services provided by or through the facilities of any electronic or
computer<B><I> </I></B>communication system, including Fedwire, Clearing House Interbank Payment System (CHIPS), Society for Worldwide Interbank Financial Telecommunication (SWIFT), National Automated Clearing House Association (NACHA) and similar
interbank payment or settlement systems, including any shared networks, internet access facilities, or other similar facilities for such systems in which the Insured participates, allowing the input, output, examination, or transfer of data or
programs from one computer to a <B>Computer System</B>. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>II.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Original </I></B>means the first rendering or archetype and does not include photocopies or
electronic<B><I> </I></B>transmissions even if received and printed. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>JJ.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Pre-Determined</FONT> Telephone Number </I></B>means a telephone number
that:<B><I> </I></B> </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">1.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">was provided by the <B>Customer</B> when the <B>Customer</B> opened the account with the Insured or an <B>Investment
Adviser</B>;<B> </B> </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
