<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Property </I></B>means<B><I> </I></B><B>Money, Certificated Securities, Uncertificated Securities,
Negotiable Instruments</B>,<B><I> </I></B><B>Certificates of Deposit</B>,<B> Documents of Title</B>,<B> Acceptances</B>,<B> Evidences of Debt</B>,<B> Security Agreements</B>,<B> Withdrawal Orders</B>,<B> Certificates of Origin or Title</B>,<B>
Letters of Credit</B>, insurance policies,<B> </B>abstracts of title, deeds and mortgages on real estate, revenue and other stamps, tokens, unsold state lottery tickets, books of account and other records whether <B>Written</B> or recorded
electronically, gems, jewelry, precious metals of all kinds and in any form, and tangible items of personal property that are not hereinbefore enumerated. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Restoration Expenses </I></B>means reasonable costs incurred by the Insured or an<B><I>
</I></B><B>Investment Adviser</B>, with<B><I> </I></B>the Company&#146;s prior written consent, to restore, replace or reproduce damaged or destroyed computer programs, software or other electronic data stored within a <B>Computer System</B>, or
that the Insured owns, holds or is responsible for, to the condition that existed immediately preceding a <B>Computer Violation</B>; provided that if it is determined by the Insured or <B>Investment Adviser</B> that such computer programs, software
or other electronic data cannot reasonably be restored, replaced or reproduced, then <B>Restoration Expenses </B>means only the reasonable costs incurred by the Insured or an<B> Investment Adviser</B>, with the Company&#146;s prior written consent,
to reach such determination.<B> </B> </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B>Restoration Expenses </B>do not include:<B> </B> </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">expenses incurred as a result of the reconstruction of computer programs, software, or other electronic data that the
Insured did not have a license to use; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">expenses incurred to restore, replace, or reproduce damaged or destroyed computer programs, software or other

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Security Agreement </I></B>means a<B><I> </I></B><B>Written</B><B><I> </I></B>agreement that creates an
interest in personal property or fixtures<B><I> </I></B>and that secures payment or performance of an obligation. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B><B><I>Statement of Uncertificated Security </I></B>means a<B><I> </I></B><B>Written</B><B><I> </I></B>statement
of the issuer of an<B><I> </I></B><B>Uncertificated</B><B><I> </I></B><B>Security </B>containing:<B> </B> </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B>This bond does not cover loss resulting directly or indirectly from forgery or alteration, except when covered

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B>This bond does not cover loss due to war, invasion, acts of foreign enemies, hostilities (whether war is
declared or not), civil war, rebellion, revolution, insurrection, military or usurped power, confiscation, nationalization, requisition, or destruction of, or damage to, property by or under the order of any government, public or local authority,
unless such loss occurs in transit in the circumstances recited in Insuring Agreement C and unless, when such transit was initiated, there was no knowledge of such act or condition related to any of the foregoing on the part of any person acting for

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B>This bond does not cover loss resulting from any violation by the Insured or by any <B>Employee</B>:
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">1.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">of law regulating: (i)&nbsp;the issuance, purchase or sale of securities; (ii)&nbsp;securities transactions upon
security exchanges or over the counter market; (iii)&nbsp;investment companies; or (iv)&nbsp;investment advisers; or </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">2.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">of any rule or regulation made pursuant to any such law, </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">unless it is established by the Insured that the act or acts that caused said loss involved fraudulent or dishonest conduct that would
have caused a covered loss to the Insured in a similar amount in the absence of such laws, rules or regulations. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B>This bond does not cover loss resulting directly or indirectly from the failure of a financial or depository
institution, or its receiver or liquidator, to pay or deliver, on demand of the Insured or an <B>Investment</B> <B>Adviser</B>, funds or<B> Property </B>of the Insured held by it in any capacity, except when covered under Insuring<B> </B>Agreement A
or B.1.a. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B></B>This bond does not cover loss involving any <B>Uncertificated Security</B> except an <B>Uncertificated
Security</B> of any Federal Reserve Bank of the United States or when covered under Insuring Agreement A, E or I. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B><I><A NAME="tx897054_26"></A>VI.</I></B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B><I>CONDITIONS </I></B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="line-height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1.00pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B><A NAME="tx897054_27"></A>A.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>ADDITIONAL COMPANIES INCLUDED AS INSURED </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">If more than one corporation, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-partnership,</FONT> or person, or any combination of them are
included as the Insured herein: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">1.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">the total liability of the Company for loss or losses sustained by any one or more or all of them will not exceed the
limit for which the Company would be liable hereunder if all such loss were sustained by any one of them; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">2.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">the Insured first named will be deemed authorized to make, adjust and receive and enforce payment of all claims under
the bond and will be deemed to be the agent of the others for such purposes and for the giving or receiving of any notice required or permitted to be given by the terms of this bond, provided however that the Company will furnish each named Insured
with a copy of the bond and with any amendment to the bond, together with a copy of each formal filing of claim by any Insured and notification of the terms of any settlement of a claim prior to the execution of such settlement;
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">3.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">the Company will not be responsible for the proper application of any payment made hereunder to the first named
Insured; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">4.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">knowledge possessed or discovery made by any partner, officer or supervisory <B>Employee</B> of any Insured will for
the purposes of Condition B., Condition H. or Condition R. of this bond constitute knowledge or discovery by all the Insureds. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B><A NAME="tx897054_28"></A>B.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>DISCOVERY </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">This bond applies to loss discovered by the Insured during the <B>Bond Period</B>. Discovery occurs when an officer or director of the
Insured or of an <B>Investment Adviser</B> first becomes aware of facts that would cause a reasonable person to assume that a loss of a type covered by this bond has been or will be incurred, regardless of when the act or acts causing or
contributing to such loss occurred, even though the exact amount or details of loss may not then be known. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Discovery also occurs
when an officer or director of the Insured or an <B>Investment Adviser</B> receives notice of an actual or potential claim in which it is alleged that the Insured is liable to a third party under circumstances that, if true, would constitute a loss
under this bond. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>BOND PERIOD </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B>Bond Period </B>means the period of one year following the inception date of this bond or any annual<B> </B>anniversary thereof, or
if the time between the inception or annual anniversary date and the expiration date of this bond is less than one year, then such lesser period. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B><A NAME="tx897054_30"></A>D.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>SINGLE LOSS </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B>Single Loss </B>means all covered loss, including court costs and attorney&#146;s fees incurred by the Company<B> </B>under General
Agreement E., resulting from: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">1.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">any one act or series of related acts of burglary, robbery, or attempt thereat, in which no <B>Employee </B>is
implicated;<B> </B> </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">2.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">any one act or series of related unintentional or negligent acts or omissions on the part of any person (whether an
<B>Employee</B> or not) resulting in damage to or destruction or misplacement of <B>Property</B>;<B> </B> </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">3.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">all acts or omissions other than those specified in 1. and 2. above, caused by any person (whether an <B>Employee</B>
or not) or in which such person is implicated; or </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">4.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">any one casualty or event not specified in 1., 2., or 3. above. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B><A NAME="tx897054_31"></A>E.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>SINGLE LOSS LIMIT OF INSURANCE </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">The Company&#146;s liability for each <B>Single Loss</B> will not exceed the applicable Single Loss Limit of Insurance set forth in
ITEM&nbsp;4 of the Declarations. If a <B>Single Loss</B> is covered under more than one Insuring Agreement or Coverage, the Single Loss Limit of Insurance for each applicable Insuring Agreement or Coverage will apply separately to that part of the
loss covered under such Insuring Agreement or Coverage, provided that the maximum payable for such <B>Single Loss</B> will not exceed the largest applicable Single Loss Limit of Insurance. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B><A NAME="tx897054_32"></A>F.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>DEDUCTIBLE </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">The Company is liable hereunder only for the amount by which any <B>Single Loss</B> exceeds the Single Loss Deductible Amount for the
Insuring Agreement or Coverage applicable to such loss, subject to the applicable Single Loss Limit of Insurance. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">If a <B>Single
Loss</B> is covered under more than one Coverage within an Insuring Agreement, the Single Loss Deductible Amount set forth in ITEM 4 of the Declarations for each applicable Coverage will apply separately to the part of such <B>Single Loss</B>
covered under such Coverage, however the sum of such Single Loss Deductible Amounts for such <B>Single Loss</B> will not exceed the highest applicable Single Loss Deductible Amount for any such Coverage. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">The Insured will, in the time and in the manner prescribed in this bond, give the Company notice of any loss of the kind covered by the
terms of this bond that exceeds 25% of the Single Loss Deductible Amount applicable to such loss, whether or not the Company is liable therefor, and upon the request of the Company will file with it a brief statement giving the particulars
concerning such loss. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B><A NAME="tx897054_33"></A>G.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-ACCUMULATION</FONT> OF LIMITS </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">The Single Loss Limit of Insurance of the Company is not cumulative in amount from <B>Bond Period</B> to <B>Bond Period</B>, regardless
of the number of years this bond is in force, the number of times this bond may<B> </B>be renewed or replaced, or the number of premiums that are payable or paid. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B><A NAME="tx897054_34"></A>H.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>NOTICE - PROOF OF LOSS - LEGAL PROCEEDINGS </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">1.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">At the earliest practicable moment not to exceed 90 days after discovery of loss, the Insured or <B>Investment Adviser
</B>must give the Company notice thereof.<B> </B> </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Within six months after such discovery, the Insured or <B>Investment Adviser</B> must furnish to the Company proof of
loss, duly sworn to, with full particulars. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">3.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Lost <B>Certificated Securities</B> listed in a proof of loss will be identified by certificate or bond numbers if
such securities were issued therewith. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">4.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Legal proceedings for the recovery of any loss hereunder will not be brought prior to the expiration of 60 days after
the original proof of loss is filed with the Company or after the expiration of 24 months from the discovery of such loss, except that any action or proceeding to recover hereunder on account of any judgment against the Insured in any suit mentioned
in General Agreement E., or to recover attorney&#146;s fees paid in any such suit, will be brought within 24 months from the date upon which the judgment and such suit will become final. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">5.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">If any limitation embodied in this bond is prohibited by any law controlling the construction hereof, such limitation
will be deemed to be amended so as to equal the minimum period of limitation provided by such law. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">6.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">This bond is for the use and benefit only of the Insured, and the Company will not be liable hereunder for loss
sustained by anyone other than the Insured. No suit, action or legal proceedings will be brought hereunder by anyone other than the Insured. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B><A NAME="tx897054_35"></A>I.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>VALUATION </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">1.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Money </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:15%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Any loss of <B>Money</B>, or loss payable in <B>Money</B>, will be paid, at the option of the Insured, in the <B>Money </B>of the
country in which the loss was sustained or in the U.S. dollar equivalent thereof<B> </B>determined at the rate of exchange at the time of payment of such loss. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">2.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Securities </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:15%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">The Company will settle in kind its liability under this bond on account of a loss of any securities or, at the option of the Insured,
will pay to the Insured the cost of replacing such securities, determined by their highest quoted market value at any time between the business day next preceding the discovery of the loss and the day that the loss is settled. In case of a loss of
subscription, conversion or redemption privileges through the misplacement or loss of securities, the amount of such loss will be the value of such privileges immediately preceding the expiration thereof. If such securities cannot be replaced or
have no quoted market value, or if such privileges have no quoted market value, their value will be determined by agreement or, at the option of the Insured, arbitration. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:15%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">If the applicable coverage of this bond is subject to a Single Loss Deductible Amount or is not sufficient in amount to indemnify the
Insured in full for the loss of securities for which claim is made hereunder, the liability of the Company under this bond is limited to the payment for, or the duplication of, so much of such securities as has a value equal to the amount of such
applicable coverage. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:15%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">If, at the instance of the Company, the Insured or any customer of the Insured becomes principal upon any
bonds, or gives any undertakings, required as a prerequisite to the reissuing or duplicating of any securities for the loss of which the Company is liable under this bond, the Company will become surety upon such bonds or undertakings without
premium charge and will indemnify the Insured or such customer against any loss that the Insured or such customer may sustain by reason of having become principal upon any such bonds or having given any such undertakings. The amount of indemnity
under this paragraph will not exceed the amount stated in ITEM 4 of the Declarations for the applicable Insuring Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">3.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Books of Account and Other Records </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:15%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">In case of loss of, or damage to, any books of account or other records used by the Insured in its business, the Company will be liable
under this bond only if such books or records are actually reproduced and then for not more than the cost of the blank books, blank pages or other materials plus the cost of labor for the actual transcription or copying of data that have been
furnished by the Insured in order to reproduce such books and other records. </P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Property other than Money, Securities, Books of Account or Other Records </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:15%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">In case of loss of, or damage to, any <B>Property</B> other than <B>Money</B>, securities, books of account or other records, except
damage covered under Insuring Agreement B.2. or B.3., the Company will not be liable for more than the actual cash value of such <B>Property</B>. The Company may, at its election, pay the actual cash value of, repair or replace such <B>Property</B>.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:15%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">With respect to damage of <B>Property</B> covered under Insuring Agreement B.2., the Company will be liable for the full cost of
repair or replacement of such <B>Property</B>, without deduction for depreciation. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:15%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Disagreement between the Company and the

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>ASSIGNMENT </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">In the event of payment under this bond, the Insured or <B>Investment Adviser</B> will deliver, if so requested by the Company, an
assignment of such of the Insured&#146;s rights, title and interest and causes of action as it has against any person or entity to the extent of the loss payment. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">In the event of payment under this bond, the Company will be subrogated to all of the Insured&#146;s rights of recovery therefor
against any person or entity to the extent of such payment. If the rules of a <B>Depository</B> provide that the Insured will be assessed for a portion of any judgment (or agreed settlement) taken by the Company based upon the assignment set forth
in Condition J. above and the Insured actually pays such assessment, the Company will reimburse the Insured for the amount of the assessment. However, such reimbursement will not exceed the amount of the loss payment by the Company. </P>

this bond, all <B>Money</B> received by the Insured from any source whatsoever in connection with any matter from which a loss has arisen, including payments and receipts of principal, interest, dividends, commission, and the like, received prior to
a loss settlement under this bond, will be deducted from the amount actually paid out, advanced, withdrawn, taken or otherwise lost or stolen. The value of all property received by the Insured from any source whatever and whenever received, in
connection with any matter from which a loss has arisen, will be valued as of the date received and will likewise be deducted from the claimed loss. </P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>COOPERATION </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Upon the Company&#146;s request, and at reasonable times and places designated by the Company, the Insured will: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">1.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">submit to examination by the Company and subscribe to the same under oath; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">2.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">produce for the Company&#146;s examination all pertinent records; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">3.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">cooperate with the Company in all matters pertaining to the loss. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">The Insured will execute all papers and render assistance to secure to the Company the rights and causes of action provided for herein.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">The Insured will do nothing after discovery of loss to prejudice such rights or causes of action and must do everything reasonably
necessary to secure those rights and causes of action. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>ANTI-BUNDLING </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">If any Insuring Agreement requires that an enumerated type of document be altered or <B>Counterfeit</B>, or contain a signature that is
a <B>Forgery</B>, or that it be obtained through trick, artifice, fraud or false pretenses, the alteration, <B>Counterfeit</B>, or signature must be on or of the enumerated document itself, not on or of some other document submitted with,
accompanying, or incorporated by reference into, the enumerated document. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B><A NAME="tx897054_41"></A>O.</B></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>LIMIT OF INSURANCE UNDER THIS BOND AND PRIOR INSURANCE </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">With respect to any <B>Single Loss</B> that is recoverable or recovered in whole or in part under any other bonds or policies issued by
the Company to the Insured or to any predecessor in interest of the Insured and canceled or terminated or allowed to expire and in which the period for discovery has not expired at the time any such loss thereunder is discovered, the total liability
of the Company under this bond and under such other bonds or policies will not exceed, in the aggregate, the amount carried hereunder on such loss or the amount available to the Insured under such other bonds or policies, as limited by the terms and
conditions thereof, for any such loss if the latter amount be the larger. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:10%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">If the coverage of this bond supersedes in whole or in
part the coverage of any other bond or policy of insurance issued by an insurer other than the Company and canceled, terminated or allowed to expire, the Company, with respect to any loss sustained prior to such cancelation, termination or
expiration and discovered within the period permitted under such other bond or policy for the discovery of loss thereunder, will be liable under this bond only for that part of such loss covered by this bond as is in excess of the amount recoverable
or recovered on account of such loss under such other bond or policy, anything to the contrary in such other bond or policy notwithstanding. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

this bond, the Company will give <B>Written</B> notice to each Insured and to the SEC not less than 60 days prior to the effective date of any change or modification that would adversely affect the rights of such Insured. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B>Investment Company Bond </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:8pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">CO-SURETY</FONT> </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">1.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">The term Company as set forth on the Declarations and as used throughout this bond is construed to mean all the
Companies executing the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Surety</FONT> Schedule below, unless otherwise specified in this endorsement. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Each such Company will be liable only for such proportion of any <B>Single Loss</B> in Item 4 of the Declarations
under this bond as the amount underwritten by such Company as specified in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Surety</FONT> Schedule bears to the Single Loss Limit of Insurance of Insuring Agreement A.1, but in no event will any such Company be
liable for an amount greater than the amount underwritten by&nbsp;it. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">The following replaces section VI. CONDITIONS, B. DISCOVERY: </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">This bond applies to loss discovered by the Insured during the <B>Bond Period</B>. Discovery occurs when any individual holding the
title or position set forth in the Schedule below, or employed in a department or division described in the Schedule below, first becomes aware of facts which would cause a reasonable person to assume that a loss of a type covered by this bond has
been or will be incurred, regardless of when the act or acts causing or contributing to such loss occurred, even though the exact amount or details of loss may not then be known. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Discovery also occurs when any individual holding the title or position set forth in the Schedule below, or employed in a department or
division described in the Schedule below, receives notice of an actual or potential claim in which it is alleged that the Insured is liable to a third party under circumstances which, if true, would constitute a loss under this bond. </P>

<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B>INSURING AGREEMENT</B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:1pt" align="left">&nbsp;</P></TD>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">2.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">The following is added to section <B>II. INSURING AGREEMENTS</B>: </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>AUTOMATED PHONE SYSTEMS (&#147;APS&#148;) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Loss caused directly by an <B>APS Transaction</B>, where the request for such <B>APS Transaction</B> is unauthorized or fraudulent and
is made with the manifest intent to deceive the Insured; provided that the entity that receives such request generally maintains and follows during the <B>Bond Period</B> all <B>APS Designated Procedures</B> with respect to <B>APS Transactions</B>.
The isolated failure of such entity to maintain and follow a particular<B> APS Designated Procedure </B>in a particular instance will not preclude coverage under this Insuring Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">2.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">The following are added to section <B>IV. DEFINITIONS</B>: </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B><I>APS </I></B>or<B><I> Automated Phone System </I></B>means an automated system that receives and converts to executable<B><I>
</I></B>instructions (1)&nbsp;transmissions by voice over the telephone, or (2)&nbsp;transmissions over the telephone through use of a touch-tone keypad or other tone system; but does not include transmissions from a <B>Computer System</B> or part
thereof. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B><I>APS Designated Procedures </I></B>means the following procedures:<B><I> </I></B> </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">1.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Logging: All <B>APS Transaction</B> requests must be logged or otherwise recorded so as to preserve all of the
information necessary to effect the requested <B>APS Transaction</B> transmitted in the course of such a request, and the records must be retained for at least six months. Information contained in the records must be capable of being retrieved and
produced within a reasonable time after retrieval of specific information is requested, at a success rate of no less than 85&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">2.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Identity Test: The identity of the caller in any request for an <B>APS Transaction</B> must be tested before executing
that <B>APS Transaction</B> by requiring the entry by the caller of an identification number consisting of at least four digits or characters. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">3.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Contemporaneous Confirmation: All information in each request for an <B>APS Transaction</B> that is necessary to
effect such <B>APS Transaction</B> must be contemporaneously repeated to the caller, and no such <B>APS Transaction</B> will be executed unless the caller has confirmed the accuracy of such information. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">4.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Written Confirmation: A written confirmation of each <B>APS Transaction</B> must be sent to the shareholders to whose
account such <B>APS Transaction</B> relates, at the record address, by the end of the Insured&#146;s next regular processing cycle, but no later than five business days following such <B>APS Transaction</B>. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">5.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Access to <B>APS Equipment</B>: Physical access to <B>APS Equipment</B> must be limited to duly authorized personnel.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="line-height:2.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:2.00pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B><I>APS Election </I></B>means any election concerning dividend options available to
the<B><I> </I></B><B>Insured&#146;s</B><B><I> </I></B>shareholders that is<B><I> </I></B>requested through an <B>Automated Phone System</B>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B><I>APS Exchange </I></B>means any exchange of shares in a registered account of one<B><I> </I></B><B>Insured</B><B><I> </I></B>into
shares in an identically<B><I> </I></B>registered account of another <B>Insured</B> in the same complex pursuant to exchange privileges of the two <B>Insureds</B>, which exchange is requested through an <B>Automated Phone System</B>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B><I>APS Purchase </I></B>means any purchase of shares issued by an<B><I> </I></B><B>Investment Advisor</B><B><I> </I></B>that is
requested through an <B>Automated Phone System</B>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B><I>APS Redemption </I></B>means any redemption of shares issued by an<B><I>
</I></B><B>Investment Advisor</B><B><I> </I></B>that is requested through an <B>Automated Phone System</B>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B><I>APS Transaction
</I></B>means any<B><I> </I></B><B>APS Redemption</B>,<B><I> </I></B><B>APS Election</B>,<B><I> </I></B><B>APS Exchange</B>, or<B><I> </I></B><B>APS Purchase</B>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B><I>Officially Designated </I></B>means designated in writing signed by a shareholder of record of an<B><I> </I></B><B>Insured</B>,
either in such<B><I> </I></B>shareholder&#146;s initial application for the purchase of an <B>Insured&#146;s</B> shares, with or without a Signature Guarantee, or in another document with a Signature Guarantee. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B><I>Signature Guarantee </I></B>means a<B><I> </I></B><B>Written</B><B><I> </I></B>guarantee of a signature that is made by a<B><I>
</I></B><B>Financial Institution</B><B><I> </I></B>whose<B><I> </I></B>deposits are insured by the Federal Deposit Insurance Corporation, or by a broker that is a member of any national securities exchange registered under the Securities Exchange
Act of 1934. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">3.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Solely with respect to the Automated Phone Systems Insuring Agreement, the following are added to section <B>V.</B>
<B>EXCLUSIONS</B>:<B> </B> </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">This bond does not cover: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">a.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Any loss covered under any other Insuring Agreement of this bond: </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">b.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Any loss resulting directly or indirectly from: </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="9%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">(1)</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Any <B>APS Redemption</B>, where the proceeds of such redemption were requested to be paid or made payable to other
than (a)&nbsp;the shareholder of record, or (b)&nbsp;a person <B>Officially Designated</B> to receive redemption proceeds, or (c)&nbsp;a bank account <B>Officially Designated</B> to receive redemption proceeds; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Any <B>APS Redemption</B> of an <B>Insured&#146;s</B> shares that had been improperly credited to a shareholder&#146;s
account, where such shareholder (a)&nbsp;did not cause, directly or indirectly, such shares to be credited to such account, and (b)&nbsp;directly or indirectly received any proceeds or other benefit from such redemption; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="9%">&nbsp;</TD>

address other than the record address for such account, or (b)&nbsp;to a record address for such account that was either (i)&nbsp;designated over the telephone fewer than 30 days prior to such redemption, or (ii)&nbsp;designated in writing less than
one day prior to such redemption; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="line-height:2.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:2.00pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B>It is agreed that: </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">The following is added to section <B>V. EXCLUSIONS</B>, <B>AA.</B>: </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">However, this exclusion will not apply to loss caused by an <B>Employee</B> of an Insured located in New York who was convicted of a
fraudulent or dishonest act prior to becoming employed by the Insured if the Insured made a determination to hire or retain such <B>Employee</B> utilizing the factors set out in Correction Law Article <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">23-A.</FONT>
Nevertheless, this exclusion will apply to an <B>Employee</B>, or loss caused by such <B>Employee</B>, for whom there is a bar to employment established by law and the Insured has hired or retained the <B>Employee</B> despite the bar. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

c.(2) above will also not apply to any such <B>Employee</B> if: (a)&nbsp;the dishonest act was committed by that <B>Employee</B> prior to becoming employed by the Insured, (b)&nbsp;the dishonest act resulted in a conviction of that <B>Employee</B>;
and (c)&nbsp;the Insured made a determination to hire or retain the <B>Employee</B> utilizing the factors set out in Correction Law Article <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">23-A.</FONT> However, such termination of coverage will apply to an
<B>Employee</B>, or loss caused by such <B>Employee</B>, for whom there is a bar to employment established by law and the Insured has hired or retained the <B>Employee</B> despite the bar. </P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">The following are added to VI. CONDITIONS, R. CANCELATION, TERMINATION, CHANGE, OR MODIFICATION:
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:4pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">4.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Nonrenewal </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:6%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">The Company will not be required to renew this bond upon its expiration. If the Company elects not to renew, the Company will provide the
Insured set forth in ITEM 1 of the Declarations, the SEC, and every other Insured <B>Written</B> notice to that effect at least 60 days, but no more than 120 days, before the Expiration Date set forth in ITEM 2 of the Declarations. If such notice is
given late, the bond will continue in effect for 60 days after such notice is received by the Insured. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="line-height:2.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:2.00pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Issuing Company: <B>Travelers Casualty and
Surety Company of America</B> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Policy Number: <B>106839603</B> </P>

<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">5.</P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify">Renewal with Altered Terms: </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:6%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Should this bond be renewed or replaced, but with a reduction of limits, reduced coverage, increased deductible, additional exclusions,
or upon increased premiums in excess of 10% (exclusive of any premium increase as a result of experience rating), the Company must mail <B>Written</B> notice to the Insured shown in ITEM 1 of the Declarations at least 60 days but not more than
120&nbsp;days before renewal or replacement. If such notice is given late, the renewal or replacement bond will be in effect with the same terms, conditions and rates as the terminated bond for 60 days after such notice is received by the Insured.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:6%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">The Company may elect to simply notify the Insured that the bond will either not be renewed, or will be renewed with different
terms, conditions or rates. In such event, the Company will inform each Insured and the SEC that a second notice will be sent at a later date specifying the Company&#146;s exact intention. The notice will inform the parties that, in the meantime,
coverage will continue at the same terms, conditions and rates as the expiring bond until the expiration date of the bond or 60 days after the second notice is received by the Insured, whichever is later. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:120pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="font-size:120pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="font-size:100pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>AMENDED AND RESTATED </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>JOINT INSURED AGREEMENT </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">AGREEMENT dated December&nbsp;1, 1999, as most recently amended as of November&nbsp;19, 2013, July&nbsp;11, 2014,
April&nbsp;23, 2015, November&nbsp;18, 2015, November&nbsp;16, 2016, November&nbsp;15, 2018 and November&nbsp;14, 2019 among the registered investment companies advised by Gabelli Funds, LLC and Teton Advisors, Inc. (together, the
&#147;Advisers&#148;) which are listed on Schedule A attached hereto (collectively, the &#147;Funds&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">WHEREAS, each
of the Funds is named as an insured in an investment company blanket bond (the &#147;Fidelity Bond&#148;) which is intended to be in full compliance with Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">17g-1</FONT> under the Investment Company Act of 1940, as
amended; and </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">WHEREAS, the Funds desire to enter into an agreement in order to meet the requirements of Rule <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">17g-1</FONT> and to assure that premiums payable with respect to the Fidelity Bond and payments by the Insurer with respect to the Fidelity Bond are allocated in a fair and equitable manner; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">Now, THEREFORE, the Funds do hereby agree as follows: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each Fund shall maintain a minimum amount of fidelity insurance one level
higher than that specified for its asset size by the table contained in Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">17g-1(d)</FONT> (the &#147;Minimum Insurance&#148;). Each Fund shall aggregate the assets of all of its series to calculate the amount of
coverage required by Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">17g-1(d).</FONT> Notwithstanding the foregoing, no Fund shall be required to increase the amount of its fidelity insurance unless and until the aggregate amount of fidelity insurance
maintained by the Funds exceeds the aggregate amount of fidelity insurance the Funds are required to maintain pursuant to the table contained in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Rule&nbsp;17g-1(d)</FONT> by $2&nbsp;million or less. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The allocation of the premium to each Fund shall be based on the
proportionate share of the sum of the premiums that would have been paid if fidelity insurance was purchased separately by the Funds, and will be based upon the relative Minimum Insurance percentages of the Funds as of the quarter ending prior to
the beginning of the first month in the period for which the coverage is obtained, subject to paragraph&nbsp;4 below. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each Fund is guaranteed a minimum coverage amount with access to the
remainder of the total coverage of the Fidelity Bond. In the event that any recovery is received under the Fidelity Bond as a result of the loss sustained by two or more Funds, each Fund shall receive an equitable and proportionate share of the
recovery, but in no event less than the amount it would have received had it maintained a single insured bond with minimum coverage. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each Fund may, at any time, increase its allocation described in
paragraph&nbsp;2 upon payment of the premium required for such additional insurance provided that the face amount of the Fidelity Bond can increase accordingly or be supplemented by a policy of excess insurance. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Any other registered
investment company or additional series of such an investment company for which the Advisers or their affiliates serves as investment adviser (&#147;Additional Fund&#148;) may become a party to this Agreement by executing a copy of this Agreement (a
copy of which will be furnished to each of the Funds) and by paying the premium for any required increase in the amount of the Fidelity Bond if the underwriter of the Fidelity Bond is willing to add such Additional Fund as an additional insured and
increase the amount of total coverage by the amount of the Minimum Insurance required for such Additional Fund by the provisions hereof. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Agreement shall remain in effect for as long as two or more of the Funds
(including any Additional Fund) are insured under the terms of the Fidelity Bond. Any Fund shall, however, have the right to terminate, at any time, its participation in the Fidelity Bond and in this Agreement provided that losses incurred prior to
such termination shall be governed by the provision of this Agreement and the amount of any return premium to which such Fund shall be entitled will be limited to the amount actually obtained from the underwriter in respect of such termination. </P>
